Periodic Implementation of Income Tax 5

— Liu

The Implementing Regulations for the Provisional Income Tax Law were passed by the Executive Yuan the day before yesterday. The income from salaries and remuneration of public officials in Category II and the income from interest on public bonds and deposits in Category III will be taxed starting from October 1, 1936. All other items will be taxed starting from January 1, 1937. The income tax, which has not been implemented for a long time, is now being realized, which can be said to be an advance in China's tax system.

The reason why income tax needs to be implemented urgently is that its purpose is to increase revenue sources. It is also because direct taxation is a way to control capital, as advocated by Mr. Sun Yat-sen. However, China can still be said to have no large capitalists to date. Most of them profit from trading and are sheltered within special spheres of influence, making it very convenient to transfer and conceal their wealth. If these few so-called wealthy merchants can evade the law, then the burden of income tax will fall entirely on the working class, which would lose the original purpose of controlling capital.

It seems easy to levy income tax on public officials and interest on deposits. However, public officials originally contribute their income to party affairs expenses. Adding income tax leaves room for consideration regarding their ability to pay. As for interest on deposits, there are many foreign banks, and most people with wealth store their money in these banks, making taxation very difficult. On the other hand, if only Chinese bank depositors are taxed, depositors can easily become foreign merchants under assumed names. If foreign merchants are taxed together, the abuse can be prevented, but it is more difficult. Because of the unequal treaties, all reforms sometimes cannot even be discussed. In fact, it cannot be without such consideration.

The solution to social problems must be based on facts and cannot rely solely on theory. Recently, various undertakings have not been effective, mostly due to the abuse of relying solely on theory. The reorganization of the tax system, on the one hand, is to cultivate the people's livelihood, and on the other hand, it must consider the strength of the entire people. The people's livelihood is now extremely exhausted, and rest and recuperation are urgently needed. Although income tax is taken from people with income, people's income in recent years has also tended to decline, especially for the class with a fixed income. Their income remains the same, but their expenses have increased. Their hardships are indescribable. Therefore, at the beginning of the implementation of income tax, it is advisable to be lenient where possible, without being constrained by the amount of income.

The implementation of a new tax cannot be without concealment, and it cannot be without reporting. This alone has planted the seeds of disputes. There are still four months before the full implementation of income tax. It is hoped that during this period, plans will be made to be as perfect as possible. Any concerns that are considered sufficient to disturb the people should be prevented in advance. Even if the abuse cannot be avoided, organizational efforts should be made to reduce it to a minimum. It is necessary to make the people fully aware that the new tax is payable without feeling that it is burdensome and harsh. This is also the way to govern with virtue.

Li Bai's Strong Statement 6

(Guangzhou) Recently, Guilin's attitude has become increasingly strong. Li Bai openly stated in Nanning that he would never step down, and has gathered heavy troops in the Wuzhou area, attempting to invade Guangdong. According to reports, since Xiang Hanping and Deng Shizeng returned to Guangdong from Guilin, senior officials of the central government have made extraordinary efforts to peacefully resolve the Guilin issue in the past week. Chiang Kai-shek has promised to advocate leniency. Reporters have inquired from various sources and learned that the main points of the resolution plan brought by Liu Weizhang are: (1) Bai will take a new position or go abroad for inspection in the name of Chairman of Zhejiang; (2) Li Zongren can temporarily stay in Guilin; (3) The Guilin Provincial Government will still be led by Huang Xuchu; (4) The troops in Guilin will be re-designated and reorganized into six divisions by the central government, and Bai is invited to Hong Kong to meet with a senior official first. When Liu was about to leave, he told people that Li Bai would definitely accept this plan. However, after Liu returned to Yongzhou, a telegram was not received until the 17th, creating new complications and raising new demands. It can be seen that Liu's visit to Guangdong was entirely to temporarily alleviate the situation. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

Draft Implementing Regulations for Income Tax 7

(Nanjing) The Executive Yuan passed the draft Implementing Regulations for the Provisional Income Tax Law on the 18th. The original text is recorded as follows:

Article 1. These Implementing Regulations are formulated in accordance with Article 21 of the Provisional Income Tax Law (hereinafter referred to as the Provisional Law).

Article 2. The income of diplomats of various countries stationed in the Republic of China shall be exempt from taxation.

Article 3. Foreigners residing in the Republic of China for less than one year whose income does not originate from within the Republic of China shall be exempt from taxation.

Article 4. The provisions of the preceding two articles shall apply only to the extent that foreign countries treat the Republic of China the same way.

Article 5. For profit-making enterprises whose head office is outside the Republic of China, branches whose business location is within the country, or branches whose business location is outside the country but whose head office is within the country, regardless of whether their capital is divided with the head office, the amount of their income shall be calculated based on the portion of their business profits within the Republic of China, and taxes shall be levied according to the tax rates in Article 4 of the Provisional Law.

Article 6. If the business locations of the head office and its branches are both within the Republic of China and their capital is divided with each other, their income shall be calculated separately.

Article 7. The term "capital" refers to the paid-up share capital actually paid according to the Company Law, or the principal actually invested in other organizations. In the case of government bonds, one-third of their total value may be included in the capital calculation.

Article 8. The income of profit-making enterprises in Category I, Sections A and B, shall be settled once a year according to the customs of each industry. For those that are less than one year, taxes shall be calculated and levied based on the income during their business period.

Article 9. When the business year changes, taxes shall be calculated and levied based on the income during the transition period between the old and new years.

Article 10. For income in Category II, those calculated by week shall be calculated and taxed based on four weeks per month.

Article 11. For income in Category II, those calculated by month, if it is less than one month, taxes shall be calculated and levied based on the actual amount of income. Article 12. The sale and purchase of goods, securities, or gold and silver currency that are not related to the main business, and whose income is not calculated under the income items of the main business, shall be treated as a temporary profit-making enterprise. The same shall apply to non-business individuals who make the aforementioned sale and purchase but do not deliver in kind on the scheduled date.

Article 13. Non-business legal persons or organizations that also engage in profit-making businesses shall be regarded as profit-making enterprises.

Article 14. The term "statutory savings" is limited to savings prescribed by government laws and regulations.

Article 15. When calculating income in Category I, the actual expenses, bad debts, depreciation, reserves, consumption, public taxes, and legally prescribed public reserve funds shall be deducted from the amount of income during the business period. The remaining balance shall be the net profit amount, and taxes shall be levied according to the tax rates prescribed in Article 3 of the Provisional Law.

Article 16. The following items of income shall belong to the income of salaries and remuneration in Category II: (1) salaries, wages, annual fees, bonuses, retirement pay, pensions, and other remuneration obtained from official duties by public officials; (2) salaries, annuities, remuneration, and other monetary payments received by freelancers and those engaged in other industries from their occupations and work.

Article 17. When calculating the income of freelancers and those engaged in other industries, if there are the following expenses, they shall be deducted first, and the remaining balance shall be the amount of income: (1) business premises rent; (2) salaries and remuneration of business employees; (3) necessary travel expenses for business; (4) other expenses directly necessary for business. For business people who use their residence as a business location, the rent shall be deducted proportionally, but it shall not exceed 60% of the total rent. The travel expenses in Section 3 of the first paragraph of this article are limited to those who have received remuneration, but they shall not exceed 30% of the amount of their individual remuneration.

Article 18. Freelancers and those engaged in other industries who have more than two business locations, each with its own independent accounting books, shall calculate their income separately.

Article 19. Profits stipulated in Article 12 of these Implementing Regulations shall be calculated at the end of each transaction. Article 20. Taxpayers who withhold income tax or pay income tax themselves (19th Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Prepares to Levy Income Tax 8

(Nanjing) The Preparatory Office for Central Direct Taxes of the Ministry of Finance has stated that the Provisional Income Tax Law and its Implementing Regulations will both take effect on October 1, and it is stipulated that the income from salaries and remuneration of public officials in Category II and the income from interest on public bonds and deposits in Category III will be levied starting from October 1. It is currently preparing for the levy. Regarding the income from salaries and remuneration of public officials, the tax amount shall be calculated according to the tax rates stipulated in the Regulations for the Income Contribution Collection Plan for Central Government, and each agency shall be notified to collect the tax. The income contribution will end at the end of September to avoid double taxation. Regarding the income from interest on public bonds and deposits, the office is currently investigating the total amount of public bonds issued in China and the total amount of deposits in various banks and firms. In the future, the office will notify the banks and firms that pay interest annually to calculate and collect taxes at a rate of 50 per thousand. The procedures for collecting the above income are easier, and the calculation method is simple. Preparations will be completed before the end of September. The procedures for collecting the remaining income from profit-making enterprises in Category I, the income from salaries and remuneration of freelancers and others engaged in various industries in Category II, and the income from interest on corporate bonds and stocks in Category III are more complicated, and the calculation is also more cumbersome. It will take more time to prepare for the levy, which will begin on January 1 of next year. (19th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The government's implementation of income tax, as decided by the Executive Yuan, will be implemented for the income of public officials' salaries and income from public bonds and deposits starting from October 1. The rest will be implemented starting from New Year's Day next year. After review by the Executive Yuan, the Implementing Regulations for Income Tax have several revisions to the collection procedures. The Preparatory Office for Central Direct Taxes is currently making textual revisions and will announce them soon. As for the collection of income tax from foreigners residing in China, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Finance are preparing to notify the procedures. Mr. Massey, President of the British General Chamber of Commerce in Shanghai, has clearly stated that British merchants will strongly support the Chinese government's legal and reasonable taxes. According to those familiar with the financial situation, foreigners residing in China who have already paid income tax when residing in other countries will not pay income tax in their home country again according to the laws of various countries. It is expected that the implementation will proceed smoothly. (19th Special Dispatch)

Appointment of Successor to Ambassador to Soviet Union Settled 9

(Nanjing) Yan Huiqing, due to multiple illnesses, requested leave to return to China. After repeatedly resigning from his post as Ambassador to the Soviet Union, despite repeated attempts by diplomatic authorities to persuade him to stay, Yan's determination to resign was firm. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has recently approved his resignation, and the government has selected his successor and consulted the Soviet government for their opinion. It is said that the Soviet government has already agreed, and the government will formally appoint him soon. Furthermore, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs intends to promote Liang Longsheng, currently serving at the embassy in Czechoslovakia, to Minister to the Czech Republic. Consent has also been obtained from the Czech government, and after the Ministry of Foreign Affairs submits the proposal to the Executive Yuan Council for approval, the government can issue a formal appointment. It is also reported that Shi Zhaoji, the ambassador to the United States, also intends to request leave to return to China soon, as he has not returned for a long time. He may stay in the country for a longer period, ostensibly to inspect the state of various domestic enterprises in recent years. Moreover, Diao Zuqian, the Consul General in Singapore, has been transferred to serve as the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Special Commissioner for Guangdong and Guangxi. His successor for the position of Consul General in Singapore has also been internally decided and will be announced soon. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) Yan Huiqing, our country's Ambassador to the Soviet Union, previously requested leave to return to China due to old age and frailty, as well as the harsh climate of the interior. After returning, he visited the authorities and earnestly requested to resign from his position for recuperation. The authorities, recognizing the sincerity of his request, have approved it. It is planned to have Jiang Tingfu, the Director of the Executive Yuan's Political Affairs Department, succeed him. Jiang has been to the Soviet Union and is highly regarded by various parties there, so after seeking the Soviet Union's consent, the Soviet government immediately agreed. A formal appointment will be made soon. Jiang is currently in Kuling, and it is reported that he will return to Hunan Province, his home, before going abroad. The date of his departure has not yet been determined. It is also learned that Yan Huiqing will come from Tianjin to visit Mr. Jiang as soon as the weather cools down to discuss everything. Shi Zhaoji, our country's Ambassador to the United States, has been abroad for many years and has not yet returned. It is now learned that Shi has decided to request leave to return to China in the near future. He will stay in the country for a longer period, and will meet with Foreign Minister Zhang to report on matters. It is said that Shi aspires to establish industries in China, and will take time to plan after returning home. (19th Special Dispatch)

Xu Liya Meets Mellersh to Discuss Anti-Smuggling Matters 10

(Tianjin) Xu Liya, the Commissioner of Customs of Tianjin, went to Qinhuangdao on the 19th to meet with Mellersh, the Inspector General of Customs, to discuss anti-smuggling matters. Smuggling south of Cangxian on the Jinpu Railway is becoming rampant. The customs authorities have requested the local military and police authorities to assist in intercepting smugglers. Due to continuous rainy days in Tianjin, smugglers are taking advantage of the darkness to transport contraband goods out of the city. Customs officers have intercepted several cases. On the 19th, Customs Inspector Spru went to the Municipal Government to discuss good strategies for combating smuggling. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) The Tianjin Customs announced on the 19th that all large items delivered through the post office containing goods listed on the customs-printed manifest must have been registered with the customs and reported by a wholesale distributor, factory, or transportation company before shipment is permitted. Re-exported goods with the stamp of the relevant distributor, factory, or transportation company on the inspection form can also be mailed. Otherwise, the post office will refuse to accept them. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) Customs has received reports that many batches of smuggled goods have arrived at Qikou in recent days, and have been transported via large carts through southern Cangxian. These include artificial silk and kerosene oil. Customs has already telegraphed the Inspectorate General of Customs to intercept them. (19th Special Dispatch)

(Tianjin) A survey of Tianjin Customs' trade volume for June shows that imports amounted to 2,251,880 gold units and exports amounted to 7,991,238 gold units. Compared with May, imports decreased by 241,000 gold units and exports decreased by 737,000 gold units. Compared with the same period last year, imports decreased by 2,909,000 customs gold units, while exports increased by 1,886,000 gold units. Imports continue to be low for items such as artificial silk and sugar. Many Tianjin dyestuff merchants are purchasing smuggled goods, repackaging them in domestic bags, and selling them as domestic products. Customs has uncovered several cases and imposed penalties accordingly. (19th Special Dispatch)

Two Breaches Occur in the Upper Reaches of the Luan River; Water Levels in Huanxiang and Other Rivers Reach the Top of the Levees 17

(Tianjin) There has been heavy rain in eastern Tianjin for five days without clearing. The water levels in various rivers have risen sharply. Two breaches have occurred in the upper reaches of the Luan River. The water in the moat and the Long River has risen five feet and overflowed, inundating countless farmland. The water levels in the Huanxiang, Heilong, and Tangshan suburban coal transport rivers have all reached the top of the levees, creating an extremely dangerous situation. (19th Special Dispatch)

Remedial Measures for Civil Service Status of Displaced Northeast Civil Servants; Examination Yuan Organizes a Qualifications Review Committee 18

(Nanjing) The implementation of the Civil Servant Screening and Review Regulations and the Civil Servant Registration Regulations has concluded. However, civil servants from the Northeast provinces, due to the incident [Mukden Incident], fled into the interior, and most of their supporting documents were lost, resulting in them not being able to obtain qualifications. The central government believes that among them are many individuals with superior learning, broad knowledge, and extensive experience, and it would be a pity if they were unable to advance. It is imperative to find ways to provide relief. The competent authorities have been instructed to formulate remedial measures for the civil service status of displaced Northeast civil servants, as well as a brief outline of the Northeast Displaced Civil Servants' Qualifications Review Committee. The remedial measures are roughly divided into three items: (1) The Examination Yuan will organize a Northeast Displaced Civil Servants' Qualifications Review Committee to thoroughly review the origin, experience, education, and usual thoughts and behaviors of Northeast civil servants. Those deemed appropriate will be certified and forwarded to the Ministry of Personnel; (2) Northeast displaced civil servants are specially permitted to submit applications for review in accordance with the Civil Servant Registration Regulations promulgated by the National Government on April 23rd, 1934, and its implementing rules. This review period is limited to six months, but the Ministry of Personnel will not review applications that are not forwarded by the Qualifications Review Committee. Furthermore, the individuals applying for registration are limited to those who served in the Northeast before the "September 18th" incident and left their posts and entered the interior due to the incident. Those originally serving in the interior who are of Northeast origin may not invoke this precedent; (3) Those whose qualifications in the Plan for the Settlement of Displaced Personnel from the Four Northeastern Provinces have been reviewed and found to meet the qualifications in the Screening Regulations are specially permitted to be issued a certificate by the Ministry of Personnel. In the Wood Management Plan, those whose qualifications have been reviewed in accordance with the Civil Servant Appointment Act and possess higher qualifications in the Screening Regulations are also permitted to submit documents within the six-month registration period to request a review. Those who pass the review will also be issued a certificate. As for the members of the Qualifications Review Committee, the Examination Yuan has appointed Wang Shuchang, Jin Zhaohua, Huang Henghao, Wang Xianzhang, Zhou Tianfang, Qi Shiying, Gao Xibing, Xu Zhen, and Dong Zhengqi. Gao Xibing, Xu Zhen, and Dong Zhengqi will serve as standing committee members. The committee will be located in the Hualin Hall of the Examination Yuan and will be formally established and begin operations soon. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) Regarding the central government's decision to subsidize the qualification of displaced civil servants from the Northeast, the Examination Yuan has organized a Northeast Displaced Civil Servants' Qualifications Review Committee. The Yuan has now appointed Wang Shuchang, Jin Zhaohua, Huang Henghao, Wang Xianzhang, Zhou Tianfang, Qi Shiying, Gao Xibing, Xu Zhen, and Dong Qizheng as members in accordance with the simplified regulations, and Gao Xibing, Xu Zhen, and Dong Gongzheng as standing committee members. The committee's address will be the Hualin Hall of the Examination Yuan, and it will be established and begin operations soon. (19th Special Dispatch)

National Election Headquarters Explains Doubts 20

(Nanjing) Li Peiji, the Chief Supervisor of Elections in Henan Province, previously telegraphed the Headquarters to request clarification as to whether people in the military districts who have taken the oath and registered in the B election districts should be considered people in those election districts and have the right to vote and be elected, or whether their original domicile should be considered unchanged. The Headquarters recently replied that all those who meet the provisions of Article 2 of the Rules for Citizens' Oath and Registration, regardless of their original or foreign domicile, should have the right to vote, and those who also meet the qualifications of Article 12 of the Election Law should have the right to be elected. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice approved the letter from the National Election Headquarters, stating that in the future, when local high courts handle litigation cases related to the election of representatives to the National Assembly, if there are any doubts regarding the election laws, they should directly telegraph the Headquarters for clarification using the fastest possible method. An order has been issued to the high courts of all provinces to comply. (19th Central News Agency dispatch) The Overseas Chinese Representatives Election Office held its third staff meeting at noon on the 18th. Chen Shuren reported on the progress of the office's work: (1) The table of affiliated locations of the overseas Chinese representative election districts has been approved and filed by the Headquarters; (2) The Headquarters has appointed Fan Jiepeng as the Election Supervisor for Overseas Chinese Representatives in Macau and Ruan Hanxiang as the Election Supervisor for Overseas Chinese Representatives in Tahiti; (3) The Headquarters has created a model for the official seals of overseas Chinese election supervisors in various locations and sent it to this office to be forwarded to various locations for use accordingly. The table of affiliated election locations of the overseas Chinese districts is recorded below: 1. Chile is affiliated with Argentina, Paraguay, Uruguay, and Bolivia; 2. Peru is affiliated with Brazil, Ecuador, Venezuela, and the Guiana Islands; 3. Central America is affiliated with Panama, Guatemala, El Salvador, Nicaragua, Honduras, Managua, Costa Rica, Colombia, British Trinidad, and British Jamaica; 4. Tahiti is affiliated with the French Society Islands, Austral Islands, Gambier Islands, Marquesas Islands, Danger Islands, British Haudson Island, Pitcairn Island, Tuamotu Islands, Starbuck Island, Vostok Island, and Samoa Islands; 5. Honolulu is affiliated with the Hawaiian Islands; 6. Malaysia is affiliated with British North Borneo; 7. Dutch East Indies is affiliated with South Borneo and Portuguese Timor; 8. Australia is affiliated with New Zealand and Fiji Samoa; 9. Cuba is affiliated with Santo Domingo; 10. Macau is affiliated with Mauritius and Madagascar. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

Judicial Yuan Clarifies Nationality Issues in Divorce of Foreign Wives 22

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Foreign Affairs forwarded to the Judicial Yuan for clarification regarding the nationality issues after the divorce of foreign women who marry Chinese men. The United Law Interpretation Conference has now resolved that if a foreign woman has legally acquired the nationality of the Republic of China by marrying a Chinese man, her nationality will not be lost due to subsequent divorce. Therefore, even if she did not apply for registration before the divorce, she may still apply for it afterward if there is no reason for losing her nationality. (18th Special Dispatch)

No Stamp Duty Required for Submitting Petitions 23

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance has stated that according to the current Stamp Tax Law, there is no longer a requirement to affix stamps when submitting petitions, and it has now notified all tax authorities to that effect. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Revises Types of Goods for Inspection 24

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Finance stated that the number of types of imported goods to be inspected is to be determined by the Ministry from time to time. Previously, the Ministry issued a circular based on these regulations stipulating the types of goods to be inspected. Now, after considering the smuggling situation in various places, the Ministry has specially revised the previously stipulated types of goods to be inspected and stipulated as follows: rayon, alcohol, alcoholic beverages and drinks, beer, whiskey, brandy, champagne, gin, sake, various liqueurs, aniline dyes, bicycles and their parts in whole or in part, rubber boots and shoes, canned foods, pharmaceuticals, antimony, diesel oil, kerosene, gasoline, various papers (including cigarette paper), various piece goods (piece goods made in domestic factories with imported rayon or blended rayon are also subject to inspection), various dried seafood products, including dried scallops (dried scallops are included), caustic soda, sugar, rubber tires and inner tubes, various cosmetics (including soap powder, face powder and incense). In addition to instructing the Inspector General of Customs and the Customs Supervisors to comply, the Ministry has also consulted the relevant ministries and provincial and municipal governments for their reference. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

An agreement has been reached on the statistical figures and implementation methods for stocks and securities. (19th Special Dispatch)

Judicial Officers and Lawyers in County Judicial Offices Should Wear Uniforms 26

(Nanjing) The Ministry of Justice has approved that judges, clerks, and county magistrates in provincial and county judicial offices should wear uniforms when performing judicial and procuratorial duties, and lawyers should also wear uniforms when appearing in court for their duties. Measures for lawyers to perform their duties in county judicial offices are currently being formulated. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

Central Hydraulic Engineering Experiment Station Breaks Ground on Determined Site and Begins Construction 27

(Nanjing) The Central Hydraulic Engineering Experiment Station, planned by the Economic Committee, has its address determined as Shoubing Bridge, Qingliang Mountain. The area is one hundred acres, and the total construction and equipment are budgeted at around one million yuan. It has been approved by the Executive Yuan and allocated from the Dutch Gengkuan water conservancy part. Formal construction started on the 19th, with foundation work first. The building can be completed in the spring. The main task of the station is to experiment with and organize the two major water conservancy projects of the Yangtze and Yellow Rivers, and to focus on detailed research on waterway flow, scouring force, and sediment content in order to serve as a blueprint for implementation. (19th Special Dispatch)

The report stating that they were free of charge is not true. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

Regular Meeting of the Committee for Uniform Road Accounting System 29

(Nanjing) The Committee for a Unified Highway Accounting System of the National Highway Transportation Committee held its third regular meeting at the Economic Committee on the morning of the 19th. Committee members from Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Henan, as well as representatives from the National Government's Accounting Office and the Auditing Department, totaling more than 20 people, attended. Zhao Zukang, the director of the Highway Bureau, chaired the meeting. The important cases passed included: (1) determining the steps for compiling a unified accounting system, (2) methods for numbering accounting subjects, (3) standards for calculating depreciation, and (4) measures for organizing existing assets and liabilities when implementing a unified accounting system. The meeting continued on the morning of the 20th. (19th Central News Agency dispatch)

German Nazi Party Provokes Spanish Revolution; Spanish Police Seize Documents 30

(London) A diplomatic correspondent for the Manchester Guardian telegraphed today that the Spanish police have seized a large number of documents showing the German Nazi Party's provocation of the Spanish Revolution. These include correspondence between various branches of the Spanish National Socialist Party throughout Spain and the Barcelona and Berlin National Socialist Party headquarters. The Spanish National Socialist Party branches were in contact with the German embassy and German consulates. Members of the German Labor Front Party supervised Spanish ports to send German expatriates who opposed Hitler back to Germany. (18th National Telegram)

(London) The Liberal Party's Manchester Guardian recently revealed the German Nazi Party's propaganda movement within Spain and the party's emphasis on the military situation in Spain. The contents are quite shocking. According to reports, the party's official newspaper in Spain published a document accompanied by a map, explaining that French troops must pass through Spain when transporting troops from African territories to the mainland. Therefore, if France and Germany go to war, Spain's strategic position will be extremely important. (19th Havas Telegram)

Italy and Germany Discuss Common Policy to Curb Communist Forces; Germany Decides to Dispatch a Powerful Fleet to Spanish Territorial Waters to Protect Overseas Chinese 31

(Paris) According to reports from the Berlin correspondent of "Le Jour," the German government, given the increasingly serious situation in Spain, has decided to dispatch a powerful fleet to Spanish territorial waters to protect overseas Chinese. The ships originally stationed in various Spanish ports will be recalled to their home country to be replaced. Furthermore, according to "Le Petit Parisien," representatives of the German National Socialist Party's anti-Third International organization recently held talks with representatives of the Italian Fascist Party in Rome to decide on a common policy for both parties to deal with communist forces in European countries, especially in Spain. (19th Havas Telegram)

(Berlin) Lufthansa has announced that since the outbreak of the civil war in Spain, it has transported 700 German expatriates from the Spanish capital, Madrid, back to Germany by plane. This special type of transportation will continue until all German expatriates in the country have left the country. (19th Havas Telegram)

The South of Spain is Quiet, While Fierce Battles Rage in the North; Rebel Forces Launch Another Fierce Attack on Irún; Part of the Moroccan Garrison Revolts 32

Burgos - General Mola, commander of the rebel northern front, recently broadcast a message stating that the fighting on the Guadarrama and Somosierra pass front lines was quiet last night, but elsewhere the fighting is continuing according to plan. (Havas, 19th)

Hendaye, Southern France - A special dispatch from our correspondent reports that rebel forces in the northern province of Guipúzcoa took flanking actions last night, advancing along the ridge near the village of Oronoz, and this morning launched another fierce attack on the city of Irún. Government troops inside the city are digging trenches and fortifying their positions, determined to resist with all their might, and have laid landmines everywhere to hinder the rebel advance. All women and children in the area have gathered at the border between France and Spain so that if the situation worsens, they can flee into France at any time. (Havas, 19th)

Hendaye - Currently, no fewer than 9,000 people are participating in the fierce battle for Irún. The location is fifteen miles east of San Sebastián, bordering France, and is currently under attack by rebel forces. It is reported that the rebels advanced to the hill where the Fort San Marcial is located at night and captured it. Despite the government torpedo boat anchored in the Bidassoa River opening fire, they ignored it. In addition to capturing the fort six hundred yards from Irún, the rebels also occupied the entire artillery battery position and immediately turned it against the defending troops in the city. Today, hundreds of refugees fled across the border from Irún into France. (Reuters, 19th)

Madrid - At present, the south of Spain is temporarily calm, and the focus of attention in the civil war has shifted to the north, where government troops are doing everything possible to protect their positions. Government troops, aided by armored vehicles, repelled advancing rebel forces near Hendaye, on the south bank of the Bidassoa River, near the French border city of Behobia. However, the situation of the government troops in San Sebastián is reportedly dire. The government troops there have issued an ultimatum to the rebel warships anchored in the harbor, stating that if they continue to bombard San Sebastián and Fort Guadalupe, all captured rebels will be executed. Last night, a large number of suspects were rounded up in San Sebastián and imprisoned in the fort, which already held more than 1,200 prisoners, many of whom were wealthy aristocrats. It is said that the accuracy of the rebel warship "España" in yesterday's shelling has improved, with most of the shells landing near the fort. According to a French eyewitness, the shelling resulted in significant loss of life and property, with as many as fifty deaths and about a hundred injuries, causing great panic among the city's residents. The residents' opposition to the rebels has intensified due to the relentless shelling. The city's civil governor, fearing that the 1,500 rebel prisoners in the city's prison might be lynched, dispatched troops to protect them. Several shells landed at the central station, only a stone's throw from the French consulate, and the nearby maternity hospital was also hit, tragically killing a newborn infant. The rebel shelling lasted for four hours before temporarily stopping, but it resumed in the evening. According to reliable sources, the rebel cruiser "Cervantes" was holed by the fort and has sailed to Ferrol for repairs. (Reuters, 19th)

Madrid - People here have recently received news from Spanish Morocco that a pro-government movement has broken out there, on a fairly large scale, and it is said to have spread to other Spanish territories in Northwest Africa. A portion of the troops has even revolted and attacked the rebel forces. (Havas, 19th)

La Línea - Arab Soldiers Mutiny; Instability Among Part of the Moroccan Rebel Forces 33

Gibraltar - It was learned here today that the Arab soldiers in the rebel forces in La Línea mutinied because they only received half of their pay. They have been disarmed and imprisoned in the camp. In order to stabilize the army, the rebel leader promised the Arab soldiers that they could loot freely when La Línea was cleared. A telegram from Tangier stated that the Rif tribesmen in North Africa are deeply afraid that there will be no food to supply the rebel forces, or are unwilling to join the rebel forces in battle, fearing being massacred by General Franco's troops, so there is talk of instability. According to unconfirmed reports, several units of the Western Moroccan garrison have also rebelled, opposing General Franco. (National Telegram, 18th)

Gibraltar - A large number of Moroccan troops from Spanish Morocco have recently arrived in the city of La Línea (north of the Port of Gibraltar). Our correspondent recently saw many of these soldiers in the streets of the city and spoke with them, learning that they are very satisfied with the military pay and treatment they receive after joining the revolutionary army. Our correspondent then went to the infantry barracks and saw hundreds of soldiers, either standing guard outside the camp or resting on the ground, all appearing relaxed and content. (Havas, 19th)

General Mola, Leader of the Rebel Forces

Various Fronts - Conflicting War News; Both Sides Claim Victory

Madrid - Currently, news from the front lines all claims that the rebel forces have gained some victories. The rebel radio station in Seville admitted that the anti-government forces have encountered strong resistance east of Mérida, while the government forces also declared that they have defeated a column of rebel forces there. The rebel radio station also claimed that a revolution has broken out at the important naval base of Cartagena. At the same time, according to news from Lisbon, Portugal, Navalvillar de Pela, forty miles west of Madrid, is likely to face a fierce attack from rebel forces, as General Franco's troops have been sent from the south to reinforce General Mola's forces. Hundreds of Spanish leftists have fled from La Línea to Gibraltar for three weeks and have now boarded ships to Málaga to assist the government forces in battle. (Reuters, 19th)

Madrid - The government recently announced that government troops have won victories in many places, such as in the Guadarrama Mountains north of the capital, where government troops have made progress. The rebel cruiser "Admiral Cervera" has been shelling San Sebastián, Irún, Pasajes, and other places on the northern front for days, but after being returned fire by government artillery, it has been damaged. Yesterday, it stayed in the port of Santoña all day, unable to do anything, and then sailed to Ferrol for repairs, but it is feared that it may not be able to reach its destination. In addition, government troops have also won victories on the island of Majorca in the Mediterranean. The rebel leader on the island of Ibiza in the west has been executed. In short, the government currently controls the following important cities: the capital Madrid; Barcelona, Valencia, Alicante, Tarragona, Albacete, Almería along the Mediterranean coast; the Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean; San Sebastián, Bilbao, Gijón, Santoña along the Bay of Biscay; and Cáceres in the west. As for the city of Granada in the south, it is under siege. The rebel bases in Ceuta and Melilla in Morocco, Oviedo in the northwest, and the Andalusia region in the south are being bombed by government aircraft, with great success. The capital has also begun recruiting new soldiers for training, who will be incorporated into the regular army in six months. (Havas, 19th)

Carbunara, Chairman of the Revolutionary Government

The Rebel Defense Committee Drafts a National Revolution Plan; Overthrowing the Current Government Under the Guise of Saving the Nation and Suppressing Rebellion 34

Burgos - Rebel leaders today are completely confident of victory, so they held a meeting to formally elect General Cabanellas as chairman of the National Defense Committee and have drafted a national revolution plan. It is said that the plan will focus on Catalonia, the hotbed of extremism in northwestern Spain, and launch a major offensive. Representatives of the revolutionary government have been ordered to find ways to overthrow the Madrid government. Observers familiar with the situation believe that this move indicates that the rebel side hopes that the People's Front government will collapse due to riots and chaos, so that the rebel forces can enter the capital under the guise of suppressing the rebellion and saving the nation, while also avoiding bombing by the air force, which would anger the public. (National Telegram, 18th)

The Rebel Side Declares that Government Troops Use Poison Gas; Violating International Law and Killing Compatriots; Intending to Request the Attention of World Opinion 35

Burgos - According to sources on the revolutionary army side, government troops began using poison gas in the battle of the Guadarrama Mountains yesterday, releasing it on the revolutionary army. General Mola, commander of the northern front, also told reporters, "This tactic is appalling. We now intend to request the attention of world opinion. Our army also possesses poison gas, but we have never intended to use this inhumane weapon on our own compatriots." According to our correspondent, the "National Government" here has decided to notify the governments of various countries and the General Office of the International Red Cross in Geneva tomorrow about the fact that government troops are using poison gas. (Havas, 18th)

Burgos - According to a report from an Associated Press army reporter, the gas used by the Spanish government troops in combat is mostly tear gas, and it is also confirmed that phosgene gas is sometimes used. (National Telegram, 18th)

Bombs Rained Down from the Sky; The Western Rebel Advance is Blocked 36

Madrid - The rebel forces suffered a major defeat near the city of Medellín in the province of Extremadura in the west yesterday. The "Political News" here reported the details of the battle, stating that government troops had long ago discovered that a column of rebel forces was heading north from the city of Badajoz, intending to cross the province of Extremadura and join the rebel forces on the northern front. Yesterday morning, they dispatched two bombers, each carrying a hundred bombs, to the location of the rebel column, where they saw a large group of rebel forces and more than 300 trucks advancing. They immediately began dropping bombs on them. Many trucks were hit by the bombs and shattered into pieces. The rebel forces were panicked and at a loss. When the bombs carried by the two planes were exhausted, two more planes came to assist in the battle, while the first two planes flew back to base to reload bombs and returned to bomb. As a result, the rebel column was almost completely wiped out. Since the beginning of the war, this battle can be said to be the most important. (Havas, 18th)

Rebel Forces Occupy a Key Town on the Portuguese Border; The Port of Pasajes is a Strategic Necessity 37

Lisbon - The "Secular News" stated that government troops in Almendralejo, fifteen miles south of Mérida, surrendered unconditionally to the rebel forces today after fierce street fighting. However, after the rebel forces occupied the town, they executed forty communists. At the same time, the Seville rebel radio station announced that rebel forces near Badajoz have occupied the towns of Almaría and Benítez, and the second column has occupied Bornos. (National News Agency, 18th)

Bayonne, France - According to news from Spain, the revolutionary army has been very active on the Navarre front in the north in recent days. Their sole purpose is to capture the port of Pasajes, because the supplies for the government troops on the northern front are all supplied through this port, so it is a must-win place. Several leaders of the revolutionary army said that the resistance of the government troops in this area will definitely be exhausted within this week. (Havas, 18th)

Spain - Labor Organizations Declare: Vowing to Fight Fascism to the Death 38

Barcelona - The National Executive Committee of the General Workers' Union recently issued a petition to all anti-fascist fighters, stating that wherever the rebel forces go, there is death everywhere and cities are in ruins. "The terror of fascism is even greater than we imagined. That is why we must resolutely and uncompromisingly lash out against it. Today, the day of the decisive battle is related to survival, and there is no room for compromise. We, the armed people, can only fight to the death with the rebellious traitors, and we must achieve complete victory before we stop." The local left-wing newspaper, "L'Humanité," also criticized reports that the Uruguayan government in South America intends to mediate the Spanish civil war, saying, "The Spanish people do not need others to mediate for them. Our only creed is that fascism should be eradicated immediately, so that it cannot be revived." (Havas, 18th)

Secretary-General of the French General Confederation of Labor: Impressions of Visiting Spain; The Spanish People are Determined to Defend the Republic 39

(Paris) - Secretary-General of the United General Confederation of Labor, Jouhaux, returned from Madrid yesterday and gave an interview to our correspondent, detailing his impressions of the trip, saying, "Spanish labor organizations are now abandoning their personal opinions and doing everything in their power to defend the republican system. In their eyes, the problem today is only one thing: the republican system should immediately defeat the traitors who are fighting separately. My impressions of this trip are very good. The Spanish people are now determined to defend the republican system and are determined to achieve their goals. The people's power is in the initial stage of organization, and there may be shortcomings, but given time, it can be adjusted, trained, unified, and used. Today, the world regards the Spanish people who are protecting their freedom and rights as the same as the rebels, without any distinction. What is the reason for this? The people are very puzzled by this. For example, the rebels' military supplies are provided by Germany and Italy, so there is no need to worry about shortages. These people are resisting the legitimate government, and the place where they launched their rebellion is not unique to Spain, but is under the joint jurisdiction of the signatory countries of the 1906 Algeciras Treaty, so they cannot enjoy the right to receive supplies. From an international standpoint, the Spanish government has the right to request assistance from various countries, but other countries are hesitating and being overly cautious in providing assistance, which is more generous to the rebels and thin to the people. The facts are there, and there is nothing to hide. How can the Spanish people not feel deep pain and inexplicable surprise when they think of this?" (Havas, 18th)

French Leftists Assist the Spanish Government: Discussing Various Effective Methods 40

(Paris) - The Communist Party previously proposed to the orthodox Socialist Party to form a joint committee to discuss various effective methods to assist the Spanish Republican government. The committee has now begun work, but has not yet made any decisions. (Havas, 19th)

The Pope is Full of Humanity 41

(Rome) - Today, the Pope gave a speech to 300 people from Rome who were going to Lourdes to visit the holy site, strongly condemning the atrocities that have occurred in Spain, saying, "The world has become chaotic, and people hate all the increasingly serious and dangerous evil things. Only with the hand of God can mankind be helped to end all kinds of sins and terrible massacres that are enemies of human friendship, religion, missionaries, and God." (Reuters, 19th)

Italy Tells Britain That It Is Willing to Maintain Neutrality in the Spanish Civil War; And Declares That It Has Not Had Any Contact with the Rebel Forces; Fourteen Countries Have Agreed to the Non-Intervention Agreement 43

(London) - According to responsible sources today, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini has assured Britain that Italy hopes that the Spanish civil war will not develop into a European war and shares the same feeling with Britain. Italian Foreign Minister Ciano has also expressed to Britain Italy's willingness to maintain neutrality in Spain, and declared that Italy has not had any contact with the rebel forces regarding Morocco and the Balearic Islands, in the hope of changing the status quo if the Spanish rebel forces were to be victorious. (National Telegram, 18th)

(Rome) - Rumors that the government has taken various military measures to prepare to intervene in the Spanish civil war have caused great indignation among political figures here, who have immediately and firmly denied them, saying, "These rumors, which are published in certain newspapers, are not only absurd in nature, but also enough to cause danger, because they will make the international situation even more entangled. It must be known that what Italy is seeking is to establish an absolute neutrality system, and to do everything possible to promote its success." The Italian government is scheduled to hold military exercises in Irpinia in southern Italy in the coming days, so it is sending most of its troops to the south. Outsiders, without investigating, have spread rumors, which is the origin of the aforementioned rumors. (Havas, 19th)

Paris - Regarding the draft agreement on non-intervention in the Spanish civil war proposed by the government, to date, only Britain and France have exchanged notes on the 15th of this month, declaring in writing that they fully accept the various measures stipulated in the draft agreement, conditional on the participation and cooperation of Germany, Italy, Russia, and Portugal. Although negotiations on this matter have not yet yielded any definite results, fourteen countries have expressed their intention to participate to the French government. Among them, Czechoslovakia, Belgium, and Austria are participating unconditionally. The Soviet Union, Romania, Ireland, Poland, Denmark, Sweden, Bulgaria, Finland, Greece, and Norway have all expressed their support in principle. Germany has just accepted the draft agreement in writing the day before yesterday, and has proposed three reservations. Only the Italian government, in addition to expressing support in principle orally to the French ambassador Chambrun by the Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano on the 14th of this month, and proposing several reservations, has not yet made any statement. (Havas, 19th)

(London) - Foreign Secretary Eden has returned to work today after his vacation, and met with Acting Foreign Secretary, Lord Privy Seal Halifax, for several hours. According to reliable sources, Eden will continue to adopt a non-intervention policy on the issue of the Spanish civil war, which is no different from the policy pursued by Lord Halifax during his acting period. He will work hard to carry out the following two approaches internally and externally: (1) prohibit the export of domestic military supplies to Spain; (2) support the French proposal to the governments of various countries, especially Germany and Italy. Germany has submitted a reply to the French proposal, but still has three conditions attached. Italy has not yet replied. The latest trends of the two countries are described below: (1) The Italian government still insists that no money should be supplied to the two warring factions in Spain. Regarding this, the British Chargé d'Affaires in Italy, Ingram, visited the Italian Foreign Minister Count Ciano yesterday afternoon and told him that it was practically difficult to implement this measure. Ciano replied that when the Italian-Abyssinian War was fought, the British government had rigorously implemented financial and economic sanctions against Italy without any difficulty. Why is it difficult only for Spain now? In addition, the Italian requirements include (A) banning newspaper propaganda, and (B) not allowing people from various countries to volunteer to join the warring factions in Spain. These two may be easier to satisfy, such as France has agreed to ban people from going to Spain to help in the war, which is one example. However, according to political figures, the Italian government still intends to delay the negotiations on the non-intervention agreement. Although the negotiations are full of twists and turns, it is better than failure. (2) As for Germany's attitude, it can be called satisfactory, because the German government has already agreed to participate in the draft agreement proposed by France, but has attached three reservations, namely (A) the German aircraft detained by the Spanish authorities should be returned immediately; (B) all countries that manufacture and sell military supplies should participate in the non-intervention agreement; (C) people from various countries should be prohibited from volunteering to join the warring factions in Spain. Regarding the first item, it is heard that the British Foreign Office has advised the Spanish ambassador Oliven to ask the Spanish government to allow the previously detained aircraft to be returned to Germany (a total of six aircraft, only one of which has not yet been released). Regarding the second item, most of the countries that manufacture military supplies have agreed to participate in the French proposal, and it will not be difficult for Germany to lose its excuse. Regarding the third item, France has also agreed to do so. Furthermore, according to responsible sources, the Spanish government's proposed appeal to the League of Nations must be avoided and must not be realized. Otherwise, after receiving the application, the League of Nations will inevitably send personnel to investigate the causes of the rebellion, which will inevitably involve Germany and Italy. As a result, the tension between the fascist countries and the democratic countries will only worsen. (Havas, 18th)

Twenty-Eight Newly Arrived Aircraft Aid Government Forces in Combat; Many Bombs Used Are British-Made 44

(London) A "News Chronicle" correspondent in Barcelona reported today that sixteen bombers and twelve fighter planes have arrived in Spain to assist the government forces. The pilots currently in Barcelona are French, Dutch, and Italian anti-fascists. (18th National Telegram)

Furthermore, our army now has the support of nine-tenths of the people of the country, but many countries call us rebels, which is deeply regrettable. Also, the British United Telegraph Company has cut the submarine cable between that country and the Spanish Canary Islands, which is also unpleasant. Regarding war news, the revolutionary forces in the province of Cordoba have defeated a column of government troops and occupied the town of Alora. Pacific Society Discusses Japanese Actions in China; British Representative Warns Japan Not to Isolate Itself; Japanese Dumping of Goods Abroad Provokes Questions from Britain and the US 48

Yosemite, California, USA: The Pacific Society continued its meeting today. Former British Naval Minister Alexander asked the Japanese representative to explain which industries Japan intends to support with its aggressive expansion of foreign trade, or whether it intends to cover up its imperialism. Regarding the relationship between Britain and Japan, Alexander denied that the two countries had engaged in negotiations to discuss Britain's recognition of "Manchukuo," and said that he specifically warned Japan that if it wants to follow in Italy's footsteps and not stand among the nations of the world, then its position is very dangerous. The representatives believed that the first way should be protection by the United States, and the second way should be joint protection by the three major powers, but the Philippine representative insisted that the Philippines has no fear of being invaded. Japanese Foreign Ministry Discusses Cultural Projects in China; To Go Hand in Hand with Economic Policies 49

(Tokyo) Foreign Minister Arita, given the strong opinions from various parties calling for a change in the Foreign Ministry's policy towards cultural projects in China, convened a Foreign Ministry meeting on the afternoon of the 18th, attended by Bureau Chief Horiuchi, East Asia Bureau Director Kuwajima, First Section Chief Uemura, Cultural Projects Director Okada, and others. Japan Dispatches Another Inspection Group to Investigate the Cotton Production Situation in North China 51

(Tokyo) In order to plan the development of cotton production in North China, the Japanese side, in early June, organized an investigation group consisting of Takahashi, an official from the Colonial Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Colonial Affairs, technician Yajima, technician Onodera from the Governor-General of Korea, and Katajo Kenichi, a representative of the Japan Cotton Spinners' Association from the private cotton industry, to investigate the cotton production and sales situation in Tianjin, Qingdao, and other places. As a result, a fifteen-year plan has been drafted and work has begun. The Soviet Union; Trial of Anti-Government Case Opens; All Defendants Found Guilty 52

(Moscow) Zinoviev and Kamenev were accused of participating in the 1934 assassination of Kirov, an aide to Stalin, and of contacting a section of the German secret police in order to carry out espionage and terrorism, as well as various actions to assassinate Stalin, with a total of fourteen counts of counter-revolutionary crimes. They were jointly tried in court today. The Soviet Russian press and public prosecutor demanded that the two be sentenced to death. It is noteworthy that Germany did not send anyone here to observe the trial. According to German authorities, Germans have no connection with Trotskyist secret agents who have infiltrated Russia, and they deny that these people are Germans. (19th Reuters Dispatch)

The agency's report also stated that if Trotsky and his son are found within the territory of Soviet Russia, they will be immediately arrested and handed over to a military court or the Supreme Court for trial.
